<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item&nbsp;1.01. Entry into a Material
Definitive Agreement.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On December&nbsp;15, 2004,
Kraft Foods Aviation, LLC (&#147;Kraft&quot;), a wholly owned indirect subsidiary of
Kraft Foods Inc., entered into two Pre-Owned Aircraft Purchase and Sales
Agreements with Altria Corporate Services, Inc. (&#147;ALCS&#148;), pursuant to which
Kraft agreed to purchase from ALCS two corporate aircraft for an aggregate
purchase price of approximately $47.2 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The foregoing description of
the Pre-Owned Aircraft Purchase and Sales Agreements is qualified in its
entirety by reference to the complete terms and conditions of those Agreements,
which are attached as Exhibits 10.18 and 10.19 to this Current Report on Form
8-K.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 10.18</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">PRE-OWNED AIRCRAFT PURCHASE AND </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">SALES </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">AGREEMENT</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Pre-owned Aircraft
Purchase and Sales Agreement (&#147;Agreement&#148;), is entered into as of December 15,
2004 by and between Altria Corporate Services, Inc., with an address at Hanger
D-2, Westchester County Airport, 180 Airport Road, White Plains, NY 10604 (&#147;Seller&#148;),
and Kraft Foods Aviation, LLC, with an address at 910 Mayer Avenue, Madison, WI
53704 (&#147;Purchaser&#148;).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Seller desires to
sell the aircraft as specified below to Purchaser, and</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Purchaser desires
to purchase such aircraft from Seller on the terms and conditions set forth in
this Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NOW, THEREFORE, in
consideration of the mutual covenants herein contained, the parties agree as
follows:</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">The Aircraft. </font></b>Subject to the terms and conditions of this
Agreement, the Purchaser agrees to purchase and Seller agrees to sell the
following aircraft:</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.95pt;text-indent:-36.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model: Gulfstream Aerospace, Gulfstream IV-SP</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Serial
Number: 1452</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Registration
Number: N603PM (as of the date hereof)</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model of Engines: Rolls-Royce Tay 611-8</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Engine
Serial Numbers: (left) 18039; (right) 18036</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.95pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All
of the above will hereinafter be referred to collectively as the &#147;Aircraft&#148;,
the specifications of which are contained in Exhibit &#147;A&#148; herein.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 37.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Purchase Price and Payment
Terms. </font></b>Purchaser agrees to
pay Seller a total purchase price of Twenty-Seven Million Forty Thousand Two
Hundred U.S. Dollars (USD $27,040,200) (the &#147;Purchase Price&#148;) which shall be
payable to Seller at the time of delivery of the Aircraft, as provided for in
Section 7 below. Payment of the Purchase Price shall be made to Seller to Account
Number [ ] at Citibank, NY (Bank ABA 021000089) for the credit of Altria Corporate
Services, Inc. (unless otherwise specified by Seller) in immediately available
U.S. funds.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.95pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-36.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Pre-purchase Inspection. </font></b>Purchaser shall have five (5) business days
from the date hereof to complete, at its expense, a pre-purchase inspection and
flight test of the Aircraft in order to determine whether there are any &#147;Discrepancies&#148;
in the Aircraft, as defined in Section 4 below. The pre-purchase inspection
shall take place at the Gulfstream Aerospace facility in Appleton, Wisconsin or
another mutually agreed upon location. The test flight of the Aircraft shall be
controlled by Seller with Seller&#146;s pilot in command and shall occur during the
course of the flight of the Aircraft to the pre-purchase inspection site.
Purchaser may retain (at its cost and expense) a third party to perform the
pre-purchase inspection on Purchaser&#146;s behalf.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.95pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-36.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Delivery Conditions. </font></b>The Aircraft shall be in the following
condition:</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\tvalley\04-14940-1\task258082\14940-1-ke.htm',USER='tvalley',CD='Dec 20 10:15 2004' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(A)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall be fully serviceable and
in an airworthy condition in accordance with the Federal Aviation
Administration (&#147;FAA&#148;) Part 91 Regulations for Civil Aircraft, normal wear and
tear excepted.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(B)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All Aircraft systems shall be fully
functional and operational as required by the airframe or engine manufacturers&#146;
maintenance manuals.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(C)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall be delivered with a
current FAA Standard Certificate of Airworthiness.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(D)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft maintenance shall be current and
in complete compliance with the manufacturer&#146;s recommended maintenance schedule
for such aircraft model which will include but may not be limited to:</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Airframe, engine, and APU component overhaul
periods shall be complied with. Any replacement items will have been completely
overhauled and at zero time when installed, with complete and accurate
supporting technical documentation, such as log book entries and serviceable
tags that verify the component(s) origin and its condition at installation.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All Airframe, engine, APU and accessory FAA
Airworthiness Directives applicable to the Aircraft shall be incorporated prior
to Delivery (as defined in Section 7 below).</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All Airframe, engine, APU and component
mandatory service bulletins or &#147;Active&#148; customer bulletins applicable to the
Aircraft shall be embodied prior to Delivery.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(E)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft&#146;s weight and balance schedule
shall be current and represent the Aircraft&#146;s configuration at Delivery.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(F)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall have suffered no
structural damage that requires an entry to be placed within the Aircraft&#146;s
maintenance records which has not been identified and scheduled for permanent
repair at Seller&#146;s cost.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(G)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall not have incurred any
reduction to either its specified fatigue life or routine maintenance
inspections.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(H)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All applicable maintenance service plans,
including but not limited to CMP and JSSI, shall be paid in full, current, and
assignable at no cost to Purchaser.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further,

equipment maintenance records and manuals shall be conveyed by Seller to
Purchaser which shall include but not be limited to:</font></p>

computerized maintenance history and any engineering instructions by the

of Conformity.</p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Correction of Discrepancies.
</font></b>If the Aircraft fails to
conform to the specifications in Exhibit A and/or the delivery conditions set
forth in Section 4 above (any such failure a &#147;Discrepancy&#148;), Purchaser shall
not be obligated to accept the Aircraft unless, prior to the time of Delivery,
Seller either (i) corrects at Seller&#146;s expense any Discrepancies discovered during
the pre-purchase inspection, or (ii) commits to Purchaser in writing to correct
at Seller&#146;s expense any such Discrepancies in a manner and within a time frame
reasonably acceptable to Purchaser. Upon (x) determination that there are no
Discrepancies, (y) correction of any Discrepancies, or (z) Seller&#146;s commitment
to correct any Discrepancies as provided in the preceding sentence, Purchaser
shall, at the time of Delivery, execute a Final Delivery and Acceptance Receipt
in the form of Exhibit B attached hereto. In the event that any Discrepancies
have not been corrected by the time of Delivery, the Final Delivery and Acceptance
Receipt shall indicate the Discrepancies to be resolved and the time frame and manner
in which the parties have agreed that Seller shall correct such Discrepancies,
and will be countersigned by Seller to indicate its agreement.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.7pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

correct or agree to correct the Discrepancies disclosed by Purchaser&#146;s
inspection in accordance with the provisions of Section 5 above, Purchaser may
terminate this Agreement. Upon such termination of this Agreement, neither

Agreement.</p>

or not arising in tort or occasioned in whole or in part by any fault or
negligence of Seller.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-35.05pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">15.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Exclusion of Liabilities. </font></b>SELLER SHALL HAVE NO OBLIGATION OR LIABILITY
(AT LAW OR IN EQUITY) IN CONTRACT (INCLUDING, WITHOUT LIMITATION,</p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WARRANTY),
IN TORT (WHETHER OR NOT ARISING FROM THE ACTIVE, PASSIVE OR IMPUTED NEGLIGENCE
OR STRICT PRODUCTS LIABILITY OF SELLER) OR OTHERWISE, FOR ANY INCIDENTAL OR
CONSEQUENTIAL DAMAGES, INCLUDING WITHOUT LIMITATION LOSS OF USE, LOSS OF
REVENUE OR LOSS OF PROFIT, WITH RESPECT TO (1) ANY DELAY IN DELIVERY OR
COMPLETE FAILURE TO DELIVER FOR ANY REASON WHATSOEVER, OR (2) ANY FAILURE TO
PERFORM ANY OF ITS OTHER OBLIGATIONS UNDER THIS AGREEMENT, OR (3) ANY
NON-CONFORMANCE OF THE AIRCRAFT, OR ANY DEFECT IN THE AIRCRAFT OR ANY OTHER THING
DELIVERED UNDER THIS AGREEMENT.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">16.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Choice of Law. </font></b>This Agreement shall be governed by the laws

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">17.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Assignment. </font></b>This Agreement may not be assigned by either
party without the prior written consent of the other which shall not be
unreasonably withheld.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">18.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Modifications and
Amendments. </font></b>This Agreement
shall not be modified or amended except by an instrument in writing signed by
duly authorized representatives of the parties.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">19.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Enforceability. </font></b>If any one or more provisions of this
Agreement shall be found to be illegal or unenforceable in any respect, the
validity, legality and enforceability of the remaining provisions shall not in
any way be affected or impaired thereby.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">20.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Successors and Assigns. </font></b>This Agreement shall be binding upon and
inure to the benefit of the respective successors and permitted assigns of the
parties hereto.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">21.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Agents and Brokers. </font></b>Each party agrees to indemnify and hold
harmless the other party from and against any and all liabilities, losses,
costs, damages, claims and expenses, including attorneys&#146; fees and litigation
expenses, that such other party may suffer or incur because of any claim by any
broker, agent, or consultant claiming by, through or under the indemnifying party,
whether or not meritorious, for any fee, commission or other compensation with
respect to the purchase and sale of the Aircraft or any part thereof.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">22.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">IRC 1031 Like-Kind Exchange.
</font></b>Seller contemplates that the
sale of the Aircraft described in this Agreement may qualify as a like-kind
exchange under Section 1031 of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended
(the &#147;Code&#148;) and the Regulations thereunder. At Seller&#146;s request, Purchaser
will reasonable assist and cooperate with Seller to effect the successful completion
of such exchange, including the execution of all documents pursuant to the provisions
of section 1031 of the Code and the Regulations thereunder, provided that Purchaser
shall not be required to incur or pay any costs or expenses in connection with
the exchange transaction and shall have no obligation to take or hold title to
the replacement aircraft.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 36.5pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-36.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

Agreement were fully read and understood and that they constitute the entire
Agreement between parties. This Agreement may be executed in counterparts. Each</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FINAL DELIVERY AND ACCEPTANCE RECEIPT</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This
acknowledges full and satisfactory delivery and acceptance of the following
aircraft and/or equipment.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

and Model: Gulfstream Aerospace, Gulfstream IV-SP</font></p>

Number: 1452</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The aircraft and/or
equipment referred to above was received by us on the date and at the location
set forth below and was determined by us to be in good order and condition and
acceptable to us.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT &#147;C&#148;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">USED AIRCRAFT BILL OF </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">SALE</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to a Pre-Owned
Aircraft Purchase and Sales Agreement by and between Altria Corporate Services,
Inc. (&#147;Seller&#148;) and Kraft Foods Aviation, LLC (&#147;Purchaser&#148;) dated as of
December 15, 2004 (&#147;Purchase Agreement&#148;), and in consideration of Twenty-Seven
Million Forty Thousand Two Hundred U.S. Dollars (USD $27,040,200) and other
good and valuable consideration passing from Purchaser to Seller, receipt of
which is hereby acknowledged, Seller does hereby grant, bargain, sell and
assign to Purchaser, the following described property (including all
appliances, parts, instruments, appurtenances, accessories, furnishings, or
other equipment or property installed on or attached to such aircraft, engines
and propellers):</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model: Gulfstream Aerospace, Gulfstream IV-SP</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Serial
Number: 1452</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Registration
Number: N603PM (as of the date hereof)</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model of Engines: Rolls-Royce Tay 611-8</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Engine
Serial Numbers: (left) 18039; (right) 18036</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 72.5pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">TO HAVE AND TO HOLD such
property to Purchaser, its successors and assigns, to its and their own use
forever.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The interest of Seller in
such property, and the interest transferred by this Bill of Sale, is that of
absolute legal and beneficial title and ownership.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Seller hereby warrants to
Purchaser, its successors and assigns, that there is hereby conveyed to
Purchaser on the date hereof, good legal and beneficial title to the above
aircraft, engines, appliances, parts, instruments, appurtenances, accessories,
furnishings and/or other equipment or property, free and clear of all third
party interests, except any and all third party interests created by or through
Purchaser or any of its affiliates, and that Seller will warrant and defend
such title forever against all such claims and demands.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Bill of Sale be

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
10.19</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">PRE-OWNED AIRCRAFT PURCHASE AND </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">SALES</font></b> <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">AGREEMENT</font></b></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Pre-owned Aircraft
Purchase and Sales Agreement (&#147;Agreement&#148;), is entered into as of December 15,
2004 by and between Altria Corporate Services, Inc., with an address at Hanger
D-2, Westchester County Airport, 180 Airport Road, White Plains, NY 10604
(&#147;Seller&#148;), and Kraft Foods Aviation, LLC, with an address at 910 Mayer Avenue,
Madison, WI 53704 (&#147;Purchaser&#148;).</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Seller desires to
sell the aircraft as specified below to Purchaser, and</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">WHEREAS, Purchaser desires
to purchase such aircraft from Seller on the terms and conditions set forth in
this Agreement.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">NOW, THEREFORE, in
consideration of the mutual covenants herein contained, the parties agree as
follows:</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">The Aircraft. </font></b>Subject to the terms and conditions of this
Agreement, the Purchaser agrees to purchase and Seller agrees to sell the
following aircraft:</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model: Gulfstream Aerospace, Gulfstream 300</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Serial
Number: 1509</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Registration
Number: N607PM (as of the date hereof)</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model of Engines: Rolls-Royce Tay 611-8</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Engine
Serial Numbers: (left) 18157; (right) 18158</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">All
of the above will hereinafter be referred to collectively as the &#147;Aircraft&#148;,
the specifications of which are contained in Exhibit &#147;A&#148; herein.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Purchase Price and Payment
Terms. </font></b>Purchaser agrees to
pay Seller a total purchase price of Twenty Million One Hundred Fifty Thousand
U.S. Dollars (USD $20,150,000) (the &#147;Purchase Price&#148;) which shall be payable to
Seller at the time of delivery of the Aircraft, as provided for in Section 7
below. Payment of the Purchase Price shall be made to Seller to Account Number [
] at Citibank, NY (Bank ABA 021000089) for the credit of Altria Corporate
Services, Inc. (unless otherwise specified by Seller) in immediately available
U.S. funds.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Pre-purchase Inspection. </font></b>Purchaser shall have five (5) business days
from the date hereof to complete, at its expense, a pre-purchase inspection and
flight test of the Aircraft in order to determine whether there are any
&#147;Discrepancies&#148; in the Aircraft, as defined in Section 4 below. The
pre-purchase inspection shall take place at the Gulfstream Aerospace facility
in Appleton, Wisconsin or another mutually agreed upon location. The test
flight of the Aircraft shall be controlled by Seller with Seller&#146;s pilot in
command and shall occur during the course of the flight of the Aircraft to the
pre-purchase inspection site. Purchaser may retain (at its cost and expense) a
third party to perform the pre-purchase inspection on Purchaser&#146;s behalf.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Delivery Conditions. </font></b>The Aircraft shall be in the following
condition:</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(A)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall be fully serviceable and
in an airworthy condition in accordance with the Federal Aviation
Administration (&#147;FAA&#148;) Part 91 Regulations for Civil Aircraft, normal wear and
tear excepted.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(B)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All Aircraft systems shall be fully
functional and operational as required by the airframe or engine manufacturers&#146;
maintenance manuals.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(C)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall be delivered with a
current FAA Standard Certificate of Airworthiness.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(D)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft maintenance shall be current and
in complete compliance with the manufacturer&#146;s recommended maintenance schedule
for such aircraft model which will include but may not be limited to:</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Airframe, engine, and APU component overhaul
periods shall be complied with. Any replacement items will have been completely
overhauled and at zero time when installed, with complete and accurate
supporting technical documentation, such as log book entries and serviceable
tags that verify the component(s) origin and its condition at installation.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All Airframe, engine, APU and accessory FAA
Airworthiness Directives applicable to the Aircraft shall be incorporated prior
to Delivery (as defined in Section 7 below).</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All Airframe, engine, APU and component
mandatory service bulletins or &#147;Active&#148; customer bulletins applicable to the
Aircraft shall be embodied prior to Delivery.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(E)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft&#146;s weight and balance schedule
shall be current and represent the Aircraft&#146;s configuration at Delivery.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(F)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall have suffered no
structural damage that requires an entry to be placed within the Aircraft&#146;s
maintenance records which has not been identified and scheduled for permanent
repair at Seller&#146;s cost.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(G)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The Aircraft shall not have incurred any
reduction to either its specified fatigue life or routine maintenance
inspections.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(H)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All applicable maintenance service plans,
including but not limited to CMP and JSSI, shall be paid in full, current, and
assignable at no cost to Purchaser.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further,
at Delivery, ownership of all airframe, engine, APU, component, and associated
equipment maintenance records and manuals shall be conveyed by Seller to
Purchaser which shall include but not be limited to:</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Log books, work cards, NDT radiographs,
computerized maintenance history and any engineering instructions by the
Aircraft manufacturer&#146;s engineering department.</p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<div style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Component serviceability tags or Certificates
of Conformity.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Copies of FAA approved STC&#146;s and 337
alteration forms.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>All manuals conveyed to Purchaser which are
subject to periodic revision shall be fully up to date and current to the
latest revision standard.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
addition, Seller will also supply Purchaser with an inventory list of all loose
equipment, tools, manuals, log books and any other associated Aircraft records
or documentation ownership of which will be conveyed to Purchaser at Delivery.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Correction of Discrepancies.
</font></b>If the Aircraft fails to conform
to the specifications in Exhibit A and/or the delivery conditions set forth in
Section 4 above (any such failure a &#147;Discrepancy&#148;), Purchaser shall not be
obligated to accept the Aircraft unless, prior to the time of Delivery, Seller
either (i) corrects at Seller&#146;s expense any Discrepancies discovered during the
pre-purchase inspection, or (ii) commits to Purchaser in writing to correct at Seller&#146;s
expense any such Discrepancies in a manner and within a time frame reasonably acceptable
to Purchaser. Upon (x) determination that there are no Discrepancies, (y) correction
of any Discrepancies, or (z) Seller&#146;s commitment to correct any Discrepancies
as provided in the preceding sentence, Purchaser shall, at the time of
Delivery, execute a Final Delivery and Acceptance Receipt in the form of
Exhibit B attached hereto. In the event that any Discrepancies have not been
corrected by the time of Delivery, the Final Delivery and Acceptance Receipt
shall indicate the Discrepancies to be resolved and the time frame and manner
in which the parties have agreed that Seller shall correct such Discrepancies,
and will be countersigned by Seller to indicate its agreement.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Failure of Seller to Correct
or Agree to Correct Discrepancies. </font></b>Subject to the provisions of Section 5 above, if Seller does not
correct or agree to correct the Discrepancies disclosed by Purchaser&#146;s
inspection in accordance with the provisions of Section 5 above, Purchaser may
terminate this Agreement. Upon such termination of this Agreement, neither party
shall have any obligation to the other or liability resulting from this
Agreement.</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Delivery, Payment and Bill
of Sale. </font></b>Delivery of the
Aircraft by Seller to Purchaser (&#147;Delivery&#148;) shall take place on or about
December 22, 2004 (the &#147;time of Delivery&#148;), at the Gulfstream Aerospace
facility in Appleton, Wisconsin or such other place as may be mutually agreed
upon, at which time Purchaser shall execute a Final Delivery and Acceptance
Receipt (Exhibit B attached hereto).</p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">At
the time of Delivery, the Aircraft shall be free and clear of all liens and
encumbrances, and shall be delivered with a marketable title and a valid
Certificate of Airworthiness. At the time of Delivery, Seller will transfer to
Purchaser ownership of complete consecutive and original logbooks, all
maintenance manuals as supplied by the manufacturer of components installed,
along with current and complete wiring diagrams, weight and balance manuals and
avionics manuals.</font></p>

successors and permitted assigns of the parties hereto.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">21.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Agents and Brokers.</font></b>
Each party agrees to indemnify and hold harmless the other party from and
against any and all liabilities, losses, costs, damages, claims and expenses,
including attorneys&#146; fees and litigation expenses, that such other party may
suffer or incur because of any claim by any broker, agent, or consultant
claiming by, through or under the indemnifying party, whether or not
meritorious, for any fee, commission or other compensation with respect to the
purchase and sale of the Aircraft or any part thereof.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">22.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">IRC 1031 Like-Kind Exchange.</font></b> Seller contemplates that the sale of the Aircraft described in this
Agreement may qualify as a like-kind exchange under Section 1031 of the
Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;Code&#148;) and the Regulations
thereunder. At Seller&#146;s request, Purchaser will reasonable assist and cooperate
with Seller to effect the successful completion of such exchange, including the
execution of all documents pursuant to the provisions of section 1031 of the
Code and the Regulations thereunder, provided that Purchaser shall not be
required to incur or pay any costs or expenses in connection with the exchange
transaction and shall have no obligation to take or hold title to the
replacement aircraft.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">23.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Entire Agreement/Counterparts/Facsimile.</font></b> Purchaser and Seller warrant that the terms
and conditions of this Agreement were fully read and understood and that they
constitute the entire Agreement between parties. This Agreement may be executed
in counterparts. Each</p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT A</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">AIRCRAFT MANUFACTURER/MODEL: GULFSTREAM AEROSPACE /
GULFSTREAM 300</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">REGISTRATION:&#160; N607PM (SERIAL NO. 1509)</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">STATUS AS
OF DECEMBER 1, 2004</font></u></b></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FINAL DELIVERY AND ACCEPTANCE RECEIPT</font></b></p>

satisfactory delivery and acceptance of the following aircraft and/or
equipment.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">EXHIBIT &#147;C&#148;</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">USED AIRCRAFT BILL OF </font></b><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">SALE</font></b></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pursuant to a Pre-Owned
Aircraft Purchase and Sales Agreement by and between Altria Corporate Services,
Inc. (&#147;Seller&#148;) and Kraft Foods Aviation, LLC (&#147;Purchaser&#148;) dated as of
December 15, 2004 (&#147;Purchase Agreement&#148;), and in consideration of Twenty
Million One Hundred Fifty Thousand U.S. Dollars (USD $20,150,000) and other
good and valuable consideration passing from Purchaser to Seller, receipt of which
is hereby acknowledged, Seller does hereby grant, bargain, sell and assign to
Purchaser, the following described property (including all appliances, parts,
instruments, appurtenances, accessories, furnishings, or other equipment or
property installed on or attached to such aircraft, engines and propellers):</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model: Gulfstream Aerospace, Gulfstream 300</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Serial
Number: 1509</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Registration
Number: N607PM (as of the date hereof)</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Make
and Model of Engines: Rolls-Royce Tay 611-8</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Engine
Serial Numbers: (left) 18157; (right) 18158</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">TO HAVE AND TO HOLD such
property to Purchaser, its successors and assigns, to its and their own use
forever.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The interest of Seller in
such property, and the interest transferred by this Bill of Sale, is that of
absolute legal and beneficial title and ownership.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Seller hereby warrants to
Purchaser, its successors and assigns, that there is hereby conveyed to
Purchaser on the date hereof, good legal and beneficial title to the above
aircraft, engines, appliances, parts, instruments, appurtenances, accessories,
furnishings and/or other equipment or property, free and clear of all third
party interests, except any and all third party interests created by or through
Purchaser or any of its affiliates, and that Seller will warrant and defend
such title forever against all such claims and demands.</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This Bill of Sale be
governed by the laws of New York State, United States of America, and</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="background:white;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>
